```demo-code jsx
  {\
    icon: 'message',\
    name: 'è”ç³»äººå·¥æœåŠ¡',\
    isNew: true,\
    isHighlight: true,\
  },\
  {\
    name: 'çŸ­è¯­1',\
    isNew: true,\
  },\
  {\
    name: 'çŸ­è¯­2',\
    isHighlight: true,\
  },\
  {\
    name: 'çŸ­è¯­3',\
  },\
];

export default function() {
  // æ¶ˆæ¯åˆ—è¡¨
  const { messages, appendMsg } = useMessages(initialMessages);

  // å‘é€å›è°ƒ
  function handleSend(type, val) {
    if (type === 'text' && val.trim()) {
      appendMsg({
        type: 'text',
        content: { text: val },
        position: 'right',
      });

      // TODO: å‘é€è¯·æ±‚
      // æ¨¡æ‹Ÿå›å¤æ¶ˆæ¯
      setTimeout(() => {
        appendMsg({
          type: 'text',
          content: { text: 'äº²ï¼Œæ‚¨é‡åˆ°ä»€ä¹ˆé—®é¢˜å•¦ï¼Ÿè¯·ç®€è¦æè¿°æ‚¨çš„é—®é¢˜~' },
        });
      }, 1000);
    }
  }

  // å¿«æ·çŸ­è¯­å›è°ƒï¼Œå¯æ ¹æ® item æ•°æ®åšå‡ºä¸åŒçš„æ“ä½œï¼Œè¿™é‡Œä»¥å‘é€æ–‡æœ¬æ¶ˆæ¯ä¸ºä¾‹
  function handleQuickReplyClick(item) {
    handleSend('text', item.name);
  }

  function renderMessageContent(msg) {
    const { type, content } = msg;

    // æ ¹æ®æ¶ˆæ¯ç±»å‹æ¥æ¸²æŸ“
    switch (type) {
      case 'text':
        return <Bubble content={content.text} />;
      case 'image':
        return (
          <Bubble type="image">
            <img src={content.picUrl} alt="" />
          </Bubble>
        );
      default:
        return null;
    }
  }

  return (
    <Chat
      navbar={{ title: 'æ™ºèƒ½åŠ©ç†' }}
      messages={messages}
      renderMessageContent={renderMessageContent}
      quickReplies={defaultQuickReplies}
      onQuickReplyClick={handleQuickReplyClick}
      onSend={handleSend}
    />
  );
}
```

# Checkbox å¤é€‰æ¡† [\#](https://chatui.io/components/checkbox#Checkbox%20%E5%A4%8D%E9%80%89%E6%A1%86)

å¯¹ä¸€ç»„æ•°æ®è¿›è¡Œå¤šé€‰ã€‚

## ä»£ç æ¼”ç¤º [\#](https://chatui.io/components/checkbox#%E4%BB%A3%E7%A0%81%E6%BC%94%E7%A4%BA)

```demo-code jsx
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { Checkbox, CheckboxGroup } from '@chatui/core';

const options = [\
  { label: 'Apple', value: 'Apple' },\
  { label: 'Pear', value: 'Pear', disabled:true },\
  { label: 'Orange', value: 'Orange' },\
  { label: 'Banana', value: 'Banana' },\
];

export default function () {
  const [value1, setValue] = useState(['Apple']);
  const [value2, setValue2] = useState([]);
  const [checked, setChecked] = useState(false);

  function handleChange(val) {
    setValue(val);
  }

  function handleChange2(val) {
    setValue2(val);
  }

  return (
    <div>
      <h3>åŸºç¡€ç”¨æ³•</h3>
      <Checkbox
        value="abc"
        label="ABC"
        checked={checked}
        onChange={() => setChecked(!checked)}
      />

      <h3>ç¦ç”¨çŠ¶æ€</h3>
      <Checkbox value="abc" label="ABC" disabled />

      <h3>å¤é€‰æ¡†ç»„</h3>
      <CheckboxGroup value={value1} options={options} onChange={handleChange} />

      <h3>å—çº§æ˜¾ç¤º</h3>
      <CheckboxGroup
        value={value2}
        options={options}
        onChange={handleChange2}
        block
      />
    </div>
  );
}
```

# Icon å›¾æ ‡ [\#](https://chatui.io/components/icon#Icon%20%E5%9B%BE%E6%A0%87)

é€šè¿‡ SVG Symbol å®ç°çš„çŸ¢é‡å›¾å½¢ã€‚ä½¿ç”¨å›¾æ ‡ä½ éœ€è¦å®‰è£… ChatUI å›¾æ ‡ç»„ä»¶åŒ…ï¼š
`<script src="//g.alicdn.com/chatui/icons/2.6.2/index.js"></script>`

## ä»£ç æ¼”ç¤º [\#](https://chatui.io/components/icon#%E4%BB%A3%E7%A0%81%E6%BC%94%E7%A4%BA)

```demo-code jsx
import React from 'react';
import { Icon } from '@chatui/core';

const symbols = document.getElementById('__CHATUI_ICONS__').querySelectorAll('symbol');

export default function() {
  return (
    <div>
      <h3>åŸºç¡€ç”¨æ³•</h3>
      <Icon type="bullhorn" />

      <h3>æ—‹è½¬åŠ¨ç”»</h3>
      <Icon type="spinner" spin />

      <h3>å›¾æ ‡åˆ—è¡¨</h3>
      <div className="icon-list">
        {Array.from(symbols).map((item) => {
          const icon = item.id.replace('icon-', '');
          return (
            <div className="icon-box">
              <Icon type={icon} />
              <span>{icon}</span>
            </div>
          )
        })}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

```demo-code jsx

    <div>
      <h3>åŸºç¡€ç”¨æ³•</h3>

      <Input rows={3} value={value2} onChange={val => setValue2(val)} placeholder="è¯·è¾“å…¥..." />

      <h3>é«˜åº¦è‡ªé€‚åº”</h3>

      <h3>é™åˆ¶å­—æ•°</h3>
      <Input maxLength={20} value={value4} onChange={val => setValue4(val)} placeholder="è¯·è¾“å…¥..." />
    </div>
  );
}
```

```demo-code jsx
        <p>å¯¹è¯æ¡†å†…å®¹ å¯¹è¯æ¡†å†…å®¹ å¯¹è¯æ¡†å†…å®¹</p>
```

# Radio å•é€‰æ¡† [\#](https://chatui.io/components/radio#Radio%20%E5%8D%95%E9%80%89%E6%A1%86)

å¯¹ä¸€ç»„æ•°æ®è¿›è¡Œå•é€‰ï¼Œæˆ–è€…åˆ‡æ¢é€‰ä¸­çŠ¶æ€ã€‚

## ä»£ç æ¼”ç¤º [\#](https://chatui.io/components/radio#%E4%BB%A3%E7%A0%81%E6%BC%94%E7%A4%BA)

```demo-code jsx
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { Radio, RadioGroup } from '@chatui/core';

const options = [\
  { label: 'å¤‡é€‰é¡¹A', value: 'a' },\
  { label: 'å¤‡é€‰é¡¹B', value: 'b' },\
  { label: 'å¤‡é€‰é¡¹C', value: 'c' },\
];

export default function () {
  const [value, setValue] = useState('a');

  function handleChange(val) {
    setValue(val);
  }

  return (
    <div>
      <h3>åŸºç¡€ç”¨æ³•</h3>
      <Radio label="å¤‡é€‰é¡¹A" value="a" />

      <h3>é€‰ä¸­çŠ¶æ€</h3>
      <Radio label="å¤‡é€‰é¡¹B" value="b" checked />

      <h3>ç¦ç”¨çŠ¶æ€</h3>
      <Radio label="å¤‡é€‰é¡¹C" value="c" disabled />

      <h3>å•é€‰æ¡†ç»„</h3>
      <RadioGroup value={value} options={options} onChange={handleChange} />
    </div>
  );
}
```

```demo-code jsx
      <Bubble>
        <Think isDone thinkTime={3}>
          <p>å¥½çš„ï¼Œç”¨æˆ·å‘æ¥â€œä½ å¥½â€ï¼Œæˆ‘éœ€è¦å›åº”ã€‚é¦–å…ˆï¼Œä¿æŒå‹å¥½ï¼Œç”¨ä¸­æ–‡å›å¤ã€‚ç„¶åæŒ‰ç…§ä¹‹å‰è®¾å®šçš„è§’è‰²ï¼Œè¡¨ç°å‡ºæœ‰æ€§æ ¼å’Œè„¾æ°”ï¼Œå¯èƒ½å¸¦ç‚¹ä¿çš®æˆ–å¹½é»˜ã€‚è¿˜è¦æ¨åŠ¨æƒ…èŠ‚å‘å±•ï¼Œæ¯”å¦‚å¼•å…¥æ–°æƒ…æ™¯æˆ–äº‹ä»¶ã€‚åŒæ—¶ï¼Œæ³¨æ„å£è¯­åŒ–ï¼Œé¿å…å¤ªæ­£å¼ã€‚</p>
        </Think>
      </Bubble>
    </div>
  );
}
```

```demo-code jsx
    <div>

      <h3>æˆåŠŸ</h3>
      <Button color="primary" onClick={() => toast.success('æˆåŠŸæ–‡æ¡ˆ')}>æˆåŠŸæç¤º</Button>

      <h3>å¤±è´¥æç¤º</h3>

}
```

## LocaleProvider [\#](https://chatui.io/docs/i18n#LocaleProvider)

åŒæ—¶ ChatUI æä¾›äº† `<LocaleProvider>` ç»„ä»¶ç”¨äºé…ç½®å›½é™…åŒ–æ–‡æ¡ˆã€‚

```demo-code jsx
import React from 'react';
import { LocaleProvider } from '@chatui/core';

const locales = {
  text: 'æ–‡æœ¬',
};

return (
  <LocaleProvider locales={locales}>
    <MyCard />
  </LocaleProvider>
);
```

```demo-code jsx
// MyCard
import React from 'react';
import { useLocale } from '@chatui/core';

export default function MyCard({ data = {}, ctx }) {
  const { trans } = useLocale();
  return <Button>{trans('text')}</Button>;
}
```

# å¿«é€Ÿä¸Šæ‰‹ [\#](https://chatui.io/docs/quick-start#%E5%BF%AB%E9%80%9F%E4%B8%8A%E6%89%8B)

## é€šè¿‡ npm å®‰è£… [\#](https://chatui.io/docs/quick-start#%E9%80%9A%E8%BF%87%20npm%20%E5%AE%89%E8%A3%85)

## å¼•å…¥ç»„ä»¶ [\#](https://chatui.io/docs/quick-start#%E5%BC%95%E5%85%A5%E7%BB%84%E4%BB%B6)

```demo-code jsx
import React from 'react';
// å¼•å…¥ç»„ä»¶

// å¼•å…¥æ ·å¼
```

## æ¸²æŸ“ç•Œé¢ [\#](https://chatui.io/docs/quick-start#%E6%B8%B2%E6%9F%93%E7%95%8C%E9%9D%A2)

é€šè¿‡ `<Chat>` ç»„ä»¶æ¸²æŸ“å‡ºå¯¹è¯ç•Œé¢ï¼š

```demo-code jsx
const App = () => {
  const { messages, appendMsg, setTyping } = useMessages([]);

  function handleSend(type, val) {
    if (type === 'text' && val.trim()) {
      appendMsg({
        type: 'text',
        content: { text: val },
        position: 'right',
      });

      setTyping(true);

      setTimeout(() => {
        appendMsg({
          type: 'text',
          content: { text: 'Bala bala' },
        });
      }, 1000);
    }
  }

  function renderMessageContent(msg) {
    const { content } = msg;
    return <Bubble content={content.text} />;
  }

  return (
    <Chat
      navbar={{ title: 'æ™ºèƒ½åŠ©ç†' }}
      messages={messages}
      renderMessageContent={renderMessageContent}
      onSend={handleSend}
    />
  );
};
```
